## modern-core-root [dartsass]

> Snapshot 1

    `/* ( a: ( breakpoint: 30em, outer-right: calc(31.25vw + -6.25rem), outer-left: calc(31.25vw + -6.25rem) ), b: ( breakpoint: 40em, font-defs: ( serif: ( l: 30px 1.1 ) ) ), c: ( font-size: 18px, breakpoint: 60em, outer-right: 200px, outer-left: 200px ) ) */␊

## modern-core-root [libsass]

> Snapshot 1

## modern-flow [dartsass]

> Snapshot 1

    `.flow, [class^=flow-], [class*=" flow-"] {␊
      display: flex;␊
      flex-direction: row;␊
      flex-wrap: wrap;␊

## modern-flow [libsass]

> Snapshot 1

## modern-font [dartsass]

> Snapshot 1

    `[class^=f-], [class*=" f-"] {␊
      font-size: var(--font-size);␊
      line-height: var(--line-height);␊
      font-family: var(--font-family);␊
      letter-spacing: calc(var(--spacing-max) * 1px - var(--spacing-max) / var(--spacing-end) * 1em);␊
      --trim-top: calc((var(--line-height) - 1) * 1em / 2 + var(--trim-capline) * 1em);␊
      --trim-bottom: calc((var(--line-height) - 1) * 1em / 2 + var(--trim-baseline) * 1em);␊
    }␊
    .stack > [class^=f-], .stack > [class*=" f-"], [class^=stack-] > [class^=f-], [class^=stack-] > [class*=" f-"], [class*=" stack-"] > [class^=f-], [class*=" stack-"] > [class*=" f-"] {␊
      margin-top: calc(0px - var(--trim-top));␊
      margin-bottom: calc(0px - var(--trim-bottom));␊
      margin-right: var(--trim-x);␊
      margin-left: var(--trim-x);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .stack > * + [class^=f-], .stack > * + [class*=" f-"], [class^=stack-] > * + [class^=f-], [class^=stack-] > * + [class*=" f-"], [class*=" stack-"] > * + [class^=f-], [class*=" stack-"] > * + [class*=" f-"] {␊
      margin-top: calc(var(--stack-gap) - var(--trim-top));␊

## modern-wrap [dartsass]

> Snapshot 1

    `[class^=wrap-], [class*=" wrap-"] {␊
      margin-right: auto;␊
      margin-left: auto;␊
      width: 100%;␊
      max-width: var(--wrap-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .wrap-left {␊
      margin-left: 0;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .wrap-right {␊
      margin-right: 0;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    :root {␊
      --wrap-width: 100%;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .wrap-each {␊
      --wrap-width: var(--outer-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    @media screen and (min-width: 20em) {␊
      .wrap-each__a,␊
    .wrap-a {␊
        --wrap-width: var(--outer-width);␊
      }␊
    }␊
    @media screen and (min-width: 30em) {␊
      .wrap-each__b,␊
    .wrap-b {␊
        --wrap-width: var(--outer-width);␊
      }␊
    }␊
    @media screen and (min-width: 40em) {␊
      .wrap-each__c,␊
    .wrap-c,␊
    .wrap-last {␊
        --wrap-width: var(--outer-width);␊
      }␊
    }`

## modern-wrap [libsass]

> Snapshot 1

    `[class^="wrap-"], [class*=" wrap-"] {␊
      margin-right: auto;␊
      margin-left: auto;␊
      width: 100%;␊
      max-width: var(--wrap-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .wrap-left {␊
      margin-left: 0;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .wrap-right {␊
      margin-right: 0;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    :root {␊
      --wrap-width: 100%;␊
    }␊
    ␊
    .wrap-each {␊
      --wrap-width: var(--outer-width);␊
    }␊
    ␊
    @media screen and (min-width: 20em) {␊
      .wrap-each__a,␊
      .wrap-a {␊
        --wrap-width: var(--outer-width);␊
      }␊
    }␊
    ␊
    @media screen and (min-width: 30em) {␊
      .wrap-each__b,␊
      .wrap-b {␊
        --wrap-width: var(--outer-width);␊
      }␊
    }␊
    ␊
    @media screen and (min-width: 40em) {␊
      .wrap-each__c,␊
      .wrap-c,␊
      .wrap-last {␊
        --wrap-width: var(--outer-width);␊
      }␊
    }␊
    `
